			    def get_chrome_version():
			        """获取Chrome浏览器版本"""
			        system = platform.system().lower()
			        possible_paths = []
			        
			        if system == "windows":
			            possible_paths = [
			                r"C:\Program Files\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe",
			                r"C:\Program Files (x86)\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe",
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%PROGRAMFILES%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%PROGRAMFILES(X86)%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%LOCALAPPDATA%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                r"C:\Program Files\Google\Chrome Dev\Application\chrome.exe",  # Chrome Dev版本
			                r"C:\Program Files (x86)\Google\Chrome Dev\Application\chrome.exe"
			            ]
			            
			            for path in possible_paths:
			                if os.path.exists(path):
			                    try:
			                        # 尝试获取Chrome版本
			                        result = subprocess.run([path, "--version"], capture_output=True, text=True, shell=True)
			                        if result.stdout:
			                            version_match = re.search(r'(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)', result.stdout)
			                            if version_match:
			                                version = f"{version_match.group(1)}.{version_match.group(2)}.{version_match.group(3)}.{version_match.group(4)}"
			                                print(f"检测到Chrome版本: {version}")
			                                return version, path
			                    except Exception as e:
			                        print(f"检测版本失败 {path}: {e}")
			                        continue
			        
			        elif system == "darwin":  # macOS
			            possible_paths = [
			                "/Applications/Google Chrome.app/Contents/MacOS/Google Chrome"
			            ]
			            for path in possible_paths:
			                if os.path.exists(path):
			                    try:
			                        result = subprocess.run([path, "--version"], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                        version_match = re.search(r'(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)', result.stdout)
			                        if version_match:
			                            version = f"{version_match.group(1)}.{version_match.group(2)}.{version_match.group(3)}.{version_match.group(4)}"
			                            return version, path
			                    except:
			                        continue
			        else:  # Linux
			            possible_paths = [
			                "/usr/bin/google-chrome",
			                "/usr/bin/chromium-browser"
			            ]
			            for path in possible_paths:
			                if os.path.exists(path):
			                    try:
			                        result = subprocess.run([path, "--version"], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                        version_match = re.search(r'(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)', result.stdout)
			                        if version_match:
			                            version = f"{version_match.group(1)}.{version_match.group(2)}.{version_match.group(3)}.{version_match.group(4)}"
			                            return version, path
			                    except:
			                        continue
			        
			        return None, None
			
			    def download_chromedriver_for_version(chrome_version):
			        """根据Chrome版本下载对应的ChromeDriver"""
			        try:
			            # 提取主版本号
			            major_version = chrome_version.split('.')[0]
			            print(f"Chrome主版本号: {major_version}")
			            
			            # 尝试下载匹配版本的ChromeDriver
			            service = Service(ChromeDriverManager(driver_version=f"{major_version}.0.0").install())
			            print(f"成功下载ChromeDriver版本: {major_version}")
			            return service
			        except Exception as e:
			            print(f"下载ChromeDriver失败: {e}")
			            try:
			                # 如果特定版本失败，尝试下载最新版本
			                service = Service(ChromeDriverManager().install())
			                print("成功下载最新版本ChromeDriver")
			                return service
			            except Exception as e2:
			                print(f"下载最新版本ChromeDriver也失败: {e2}")
			                # 最后尝试使用Chrome Dev Channel
			                try:
			                    service = Service(ChromeDriverManager(chrome_type=ChromeType.CHROMIUM).install())
			                    print("成功下载Chrome Dev Channel Driver")
			                    return service
			                except Exception as e3:
			                    print(f"Chrome Dev Channel Driver下载也失败: {e3}")
			                    raise e3
			
			    def check_chrome_path():
			        """检查Chrome浏览器路径"""
			        system = platform.system().lower()
			        possible_paths = []
			        
			        if system == "windows":
			            possible_paths = [
			                r"C:\Program Files\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe",
			                r"C:\Program Files (x86)\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe",
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%PROGRAMFILES%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%PROGRAMFILES(X86)%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                os.path.expandvars(r"%LOCALAPPDATA%\Google\Chrome\Application\chrome.exe"),
			                r"C:\Program Files\Google\Chrome Dev\Application\chrome.exe",  # Chrome Dev版本
			                r"C:\Program Files (x86)\Google\Chrome Dev\Application\chrome.exe"
			            ]
			        elif system == "darwin":  # macOS
			            possible_paths = [
			                "/Applications/Google Chrome.app/Contents/MacOS/Google Chrome"
			            ]
			        else:  # Linux
			            possible_paths = [
			                "/usr/bin/google-chrome",
			                "/usr/bin/chromium-browser"
			            ]
			        
			        for path in possible_paths:
			            if os.path.exists(path):
			                return path
			        return None
			
			    def search(word,txt_entry,process_function,process_b_id,i,j):
			        global driver,text,collect_link
			        result_text = ""  # 收集所有输出的字符串变量
			        
			        with driver_lock:  # 使用锁保护driver访问
			            if driver is None:
			                error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因: AI浏览器未初始化，请先执行AI初始化操作\n'
			                result_text += error_msg
			                return result_text
			        
			        try:
			            url = f'https://chat.baidu.com/search?&dyTabStr=MCwxMiwzLDEsMiwxMyw3LDYsNSw5&pd=csaitab&setype=csaitab&extParamsJson=%7B%22enter_type%22%3A%22search_a_tab%22%2C%22sa%22%3A%22vs_tab%22%2C%22apagelid%22%3A%229405376116451188355%22%2C%22ori_lid%22%3A%229405376116451188355%22%7D'
			            
			            with driver_lock:  # 使用锁保护driver访问
			                # 插入文本内容
			                driver.get(url)  # 打开网页
			                input_element = driver.find_element(By.ID, "chat-textarea")
			                input_element.send_keys('请仅以纯文本形式回复，不要使用任何格式化语法，每段至少有一行纯文本回答。' + str(word))
			
			                # 模拟回车键提交
			                input_element.send_keys(Keys.RETURN)  # 刷新让其显示
			
			            try:
			                # 等待第一个AI段落出现
			                try:
			                    WebDriverWait(driver, 25, 0.3).until(
			                        # 使用稳定的选择器
			                        # class=这种最精确，不是只要包含这个元素名就行
			                        EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='marklang-paragraph']"))
			                    )
			                except Exception as e:
			                    error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                    result_text += error_msg
			                    return result_text
			                    
			                try:
			                    # 等待至少2个段落出现（确保其内容完整，避免遗漏）使用最强大的python选择器
			                    WebDriverWait(driver, 180, 0.3).until(
			                        lambda d: len(d.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='marklang']")) >= 1
			                    )
			                except Exception as e:
			                    error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                    result_text += error_msg
			                    return result_text
			                    
			                # 检查是否全部生成出来
			                try:
			                    WebDriverWait(driver, 300, 0.3).until(
			                        # until只能有一个等待值但是any_of/all_of可以有多个
			                        EC.all_of(
			                            # 使用稳定的选择器
			                            # class=这种最精确，不是只要包含这个元素名就行
			                            # class*=这种只要部分达标即可可以防止因网页代码更新造成的错误
			                            EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='cos-icon cos-icon-exchange']")),
			                        )
			                    )
			                except Exception as e:
			                    error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                    result_text += error_msg
			                    return result_text
			                    
			                # 滚动到底部，触发所有内容渲染
			                with driver_lock:  # 使用锁保护driver访问
			                    driver.execute_script("window.scrollTo(0, document.body.scrollHeight);")
			                    # 使用 Selenium 直接查找所有 AI 段落
			                    # 关闭深度思考打印部分
			                    parent_elements = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR,"[class*='ai-entry-block adjust-layout ai-markdown']")
			                    # div中提取为列表形式
			                    paragraphs = []
			                    # 遍历每个父元素，从中查找段落
			                    for parent in parent_elements:
			                        try:
			                            child_paragraphs = parent.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='marklang-paragraph']")
			                            paragraphs.extend(child_paragraphs)  # 将所有元素组合到一起
			                        except:
			                            continue
			                        else:
			                            paragraphs = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='marklang-paragraph']")
			                            # 遍历并输出每一段内容
			                            for idx, p in enumerate(paragraphs, 0):
			                                try:
			                                    text_word = p.text.strip()  # 去除首尾空白字符
			                                    if text_word:  # 避免输出空段落
			                                        paragraph_text = f'{text_word}\n'
			                                        result_text += paragraph_text
			                                except Exception as e:
			                                    error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                                    result_text += error_msg
			                                    
			                    try:
			                        # 找到包含内容的元素
			                        container = driver.find_element(By.CLASS_NAME, "marklang")
			                        # 提取所有 li 元素的文本
			                        list_items = container.find_elements(By.TAG_NAME, "li")
			                        for idx, li in enumerate(list_items, 1):
			                            text_word = li.text.strip()  # 使用 .text 属性获取可见文本
			                            list_text = f'{text_word}\n'
			                            result_text += list_text
			                    except:
			                        pass
			                        
			                    try:
			                        # 有多张class=x的图片
			                        images = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "[class*='_chat-guide-tooltip']")
			                        # 遍历并输出每一张图片
			                        for j_idx, image in enumerate(images, 0):
			                            # 有多张class=x的图片
			                            image_elements = image.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "img[class*='_image-visible']")
			                            # 防止元素过期
			                            for z, img in enumerate(image_elements, 0):
			                                # attribute属性
			                                img_src = img.get_attribute("src")
			                                if img_src and not img_src.startswith("data:"):  # 过滤 base64 占位图
			                                    try:
			                                        response = requests.get(img_src, timeout=10)
			                                        img_data = BytesIO(response.content)  # 将内容载入内存流
			                                        img = Image.open(img_data)
			                                        # 调整图片大小（可选，避免过大）
			                                        img.thumbnail((270, 270))  # 最大宽高 270px
			                                        img_tk = ImageTk.PhotoImage(img)
			
			                                        # 为每张图片创建唯一的链接ID
			                                        unique_img_id = f"ai_img_{j_idx}_{z}_{collect_link}"
			
			                                        # 在 Tkinter 文本框中显示图片
			                                        if len(str(img_src)) > 33:
			                                            img_src_complete = img_src
			                                            img_src = img_src[0:33]
			                                        
			                                        img_text = f"\n图片:\n{img_src}\n\n\n\n"
			                                        result_text += img_text
			                                        
			                                        # 修正：使用列表保存所有图片引用，而不是覆盖单个变量
			                                        if not hasattr(txt_entry, 'image_list'):
			                                            txt_entry.image_list = []
			                                        txt_entry.image_list.append(img_tk)  # 保存引用到列表，防止垃圾回收
			                                    except Exception as e:
			                                        error_response = response.raise_for_status()  # 抛出 HTTP 错误（如 404、500）
			                                        error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                                        result_text += error_msg
			                    except Exception as e:
			                        error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                        result_text += error_msg
			            except Exception as e:
			                error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			                result_text += error_msg
			                
			            separator_text = f'\n--------------------------\n\n'
			            result_text += separator_text
			            
			        except Exception as e:
			            error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n'
			            result_text += error_msg
			            
			        return result_text
			
			    def DESTROY():
			        global driver
			        with driver_lock:  # 使用锁保护driver访问
			            if driver:
			                try:
			                    driver.quit()
			                    driver = None
			                except:
			                    pass
			
			    def deployment(place,version,i,j,process_b_id_i_j,process_function,process_b_id):
			        global driver
			        try:
			            # 检测Chrome版本和路径
			            detected_version, detected_path = get_chrome_version()
			            
			            if detected_version:
			                #print(f"检测到Chrome版本: {detected_version}, 路径: {detected_path}")
			                chrome_path = detected_path
			            else:
			                # 如果无法检测版本，使用原来的方式
			                chrome_path = place if place and place != '浏览器地址' else check_chrome_path()
			                
			                if not chrome_path or chrome_path == '浏览器地址':
			                    # 尝试使用系统PATH中的Chrome
			                    try:
			                        if platform.system() == "Windows":
			                            result = subprocess.run(['where', 'chrome'], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                            if result.returncode != 0:
			                                result = subprocess.run(['where', 'googlechrome'], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                        else:
			                            result = subprocess.run(['which', 'google-chrome'], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                            if result.returncode != 0:
			                                result = subprocess.run(['which', 'chromium-browser'], capture_output=True, text=True)
			                        
			                        if result.returncode == 0:
			                            chrome_path = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')[0]
			                    except:
			                        pass
			                
			                if not chrome_path:
			                    error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][0]}\n错误原因: 无法找到Chrome浏览器，请确认已安装Chrome浏览器\n'
			                    return error_msg
			            
			            #print(f"使用Chrome路径: {chrome_path}")
			            
			            chrome_options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
			            chrome_options.binary_location = chrome_path
			            
			            # 添加更多兼容性选项
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-dev-shm-usage')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-gpu')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--remote-debugging-port=9222')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-extensions')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-plugins-discovery')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-background-timer-throttling')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-renderer-backgrounding')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-backgrounding-occluded-windows')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-ipc-flooding-protection')
			            chrome_options.add_argument('--disable-background-networking')
			            chrome_options.add_experimental_option("excludeSwitches", ["enable-automation"])
			            chrome_options.add_experimental_option('useAutomationExtension', False)
			            chrome_options.add_argument("--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled")
			            
			            # 设置页面加载策略
			            chrome_options.page_load_strategy = 'eager'
			            
			            # 下载匹配版本的ChromeDriver
			            try:
			                if detected_version:
			                    service = download_chromedriver_for_version(detected_version)
			                else:
			                    # 如果无法检测版本，使用默认方式
			                    service = Service(ChromeDriverManager().install())
			            except Exception as e:
			                #print(f"ChromeDriver下载失败: {e}")
			                # 最后尝试使用系统PATH中的chromedriver
			                service = Service()  # 使用系统PATH中的chromedriver
			            
			            # 创建WebDriver实例
			            with driver_lock:  # 使用锁保护driver访问
			                driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service, options=chrome_options)
			                
			                # 执行脚本隐藏自动化特征
			                driver.execute_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
			                
			                #print("Chrome浏览器启动成功")
			                
			                # 访问AI聊天页面
			                url = 'https://chat.baidu.com/search?&dyTabStr=MCwxMiwzLDEsMiwxMyw3LDYsNSw5&pd=csaitab&setype=csaitab&extParamsJson=%7B%22enter_type%22%3A%22search_a_tab%22%2C%22sa%22%3A%22vs_tab%22%2C%22apagelid%22%3A%229405376116451188355%22%2C%22ori_lid%22%3A%229405376116451188355%22%7D'
			                driver.get(url)
			                
			                # 设置隐式等待
			                driver.implicitly_wait(10)
			            
			            return f'AI初始化成功，浏览器路径: {chrome_path[-50:] if len(chrome_path) > 50 else chrome_path}\n检测到的Chrome版本: {detected_version or "未知"}'
			        except Exception as e:
			            error_msg = f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][0]}\n错误原因: {str(e)}\n'
			            error_msg += '请检查Chrome浏览器版本是否过新，可能需要更新ChromeDriver或使用稳定版Chrome浏览器\n'
			            return error_msg

			    PluginB = tk.Tk()
			    main_title='PET 插件块 [1.1.3]'
			    style = ttk.Style()
			    style.configure('TButton', font=('微软雅黑', 9),padding=(5,6, 5, 6))#padding 的第2、4个值控制垂直内边距，数值越大按钮越高

			    PluginB.title(f'{main_title}')
			
			    # 创建一个垂直的PanedWindow来包含上下两部分
			    vertical_paned = ttk.PanedWindow(PluginB, orient=tk.VERTICAL)
			    vertical_paned.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=2, pady=2)
			
			    # 上方容器窗口(左侧子窗口 右侧子窗口) - 作为上半部分
			    paned_window = ttk.PanedWindow(vertical_paned, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL)
			    # 不要直接pack，而是添加到垂直PanedWindow中
			    # 左侧子窗口
			    left_frame = ttk.Frame(paned_window, relief=tk.RAISED)
			    paned_window.add(left_frame, weight=3)
			    left_frame.pack_propagate(False)  # 防止子控件撑大框架
			    # 右侧子窗口
			    right_frame = ttk.Frame(paned_window, relief="sunken")
			    paned_window.add(right_frame, weight=10)
			    # 添加上半部分到垂直PanedWindow
			    vertical_paned.add(paned_window, weight=3)  # weight表示初始相对大小
			
			
			    # # 下方容器窗口 - 作为下半部分
			    bottom_window = ttk.Frame(vertical_paned, relief='sunken')
			    bottom_window.pack_propagate(False)  # 防止子控件撑大框架
			    # 不要直接pack，而是添加到垂直PanedWindow中
			    vertical_paned.add(bottom_window, weight=1)  # weight表示初始相对大小
			
			
			    repeat_id = ''  # 保留原变量
			    button_place = {}  # 保留原变量
			    button_id = -1  # 保留原变量
			    printff = []  # 保留原变量
			    entry_control=[]
			    style = ttk.Style()
			
			    left_frame_color='#F2F2F2'
			    right_frame_color='#F2F2F2'
			    bottom_frame_color='#F2F2F2'
			    def window_color_r(color_r):
			        global right_frame_color,text_frame_List
			        right_frame_color = color_r
			        for i in range(len(text_frame_List)):
			            text_frame_List[i].configure(bg=f'{color_r}')
			        style.configure('Greenright.TFrame',background=f'{color_r}')
			        right_frame.configure(style='Greenright.TFrame')
			    def window_color_l(color_l):
			        global left_frame_color
			        left_frame_color = color_l
			        style.configure('Greenleft.TFrame',background=f'{color_l}')
			        left_frame.configure(style='Greenleft.TFrame')
			        txt_insert.config(bg=f'{color_l}')
			    def window_color_b(color_b):
			        global bottom_frame_color
			        bottom_frame_color = color_b
			        style.configure('Greenbottom.TFrame',background=f'{color_b}')
			        bottom_window.configure(style='Greenbottom.TFrame')
			        txt_entry.config(bg=f'{color_b}')
			
			    def exchange():
			        return
			    # 创建菜单栏
			    menu_bar = tk.Menu(PluginB)

			    file_menu = tk.Menu(menu_bar, tearoff=0)
			    file_menu2 = tk.Menu(menu_bar, tearoff=0)

			    file_menu.add_command(label="退出项目", state='disabled',command=exchange)
			    file_menu.add_separator()
			    file_menu.add_command(label="保存", state='disabled',command=exchange)
			    file_menu.add_command(label="另存为", state='disabled',command=exchange)
			    file_menu.add_command(label='撤回',state='disabled',command=exchange)
			
			    file_menuu=tk.Menu(file_menuu_z,tearoff=0)

			    def ERROR(i,j,e):
			        global txt_entry
			        txt_entry.tag_config('error', foreground='#FF6A6A')
			        txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			        txt_entry.insert(tk.END,
			                         f'发生错误: 第{i}项 ,第{j}块 插件块 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}\n错误原因:{e}\n',
			                         'error')
			        txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			    弹窗=None
			    def make_text(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global process_function,process_b_id,弹窗,txt_entry
			        try:
			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			            txt_entry.insert(tk.END, '尝试生成标签\n')
			            PluginB.update()
			            弹窗=tk.Toplevel(PluginB)  # PluginB需是主窗口引用
			            弹窗.title(f'插件块 生成标签')
			            弹窗.attributes('-topmost', True)
			            # 设置窗口的初始位置（右下角坐标）
			            def place_window_to_bottom_right(root, window_width=360, window_height=220):
			                # 获取屏幕的宽度和高度
			                screen_width = root.winfo_screenwidth()
			                screen_height = root.winfo_screenheight()
			
			                # 计算窗口左上角的坐标
			                x_coordinate = screen_width - window_width - 24  # 从右侧留出一点空间
			                y_coordinate = screen_height - window_height - 113  # 从底部留出一点空间（考虑到任务栏）
			
			                # 设置窗口的大小和位置
			                弹窗.geometry(
			                    f"{window_width}x{window_height}+{x_coordinate}+{y_coordinate}")
			
			            # 使用函数将窗口放置到右下角
			            place_window_to_bottom_right(弹窗)
			            # 使用 ttk 创建一个框架
			            frame = ttk.Frame(弹窗, padding="10 10 10 10")
			            frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True)
			            # 添加一个标签
			            label = ttk.Label(frame, text=f"{process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]}", font=("微软雅黑", 13, "bold"))
			            label.place(x=3, y=38)
			            txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			            PluginB.update()
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i,j,e)
			    def move_mouse(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global process_function,process_b_id,txt_entry

			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')

			                             f'正在移动鼠标至: x={x} , y={y}\n', )
			            PluginB.update()
			            pyautogui.moveTo(int(process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]),int(process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][2]), 0.3)
			            txt_entry.insert(tk.END, '完成移动\n')
			            txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			            PluginB.update()
			
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i, j, e)

			    click_check_yn=None
			    # 存储已绑定的按键，避免重复绑定
			    bound_keys = set()
			    #click_id_p=None
			    click_id_i=None
			    change_yn=None
			    j=0
			    def click_check(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global click_check_yn, bound_keys,txt_entry
			        try:
			            if click_check_yn==False:
			                click_check_yn=False
			                return
			            else:click_check_yn=True
			            def on_special_key(event):
			                global click_check_yn,click_id_i,bound_keys
			                txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'监听到 {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]}...\n')
			                click_check_yn = False
			                PluginB.update()
			                txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                PluginB.unbind_all(f'<{target_key}>')
			                bound_keys.remove(target_key)
			                PlunB_running(click_id_i)
			                click_id_i=None
			            # 获取要监听的按键
			            target_key = process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]
			            # 避免重复绑定
			            if target_key not in bound_keys:
			                PluginB.bind_all(f'<{target_key}>', on_special_key)
			                bound_keys.add(target_key)
			            PluginB.after(500,lambda:click_check(process_b_id_i_j,i,j))
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i, j, e)
			    click_check_yn_t=None
			    click_id_i_t=None
			    def time_check_wait(process_b_id_i_j,i_i,j_j):
			        global  click_id_i_t,txt_entry,j,click_check_yn_t
			        try:
			            if click_check_yn_t==False:
			                    return
			            else:click_check_yn_t=True
			            current_time=datetime.now()
			            hour=f'{current_time.hour: 02d}'
			            minute=f'{current_time.minute: 02d}'
			            if int(hour)==int(process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]) and int(minute)==int(process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][2]):
			                txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'检测到当前 {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]} : {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][2]}...\n')
			                click_check_yn_t = False
			                PluginB.update()
			                txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                j+=1
			                PlunB_running(click_id_i_t)
			                click_id_i_t = None
			                return
			            PluginB.after(500,lambda:time_check_wait(process_b_id_i_j,i_i,j_j))
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i_i, j_j, e)
			
			
			    def INVOKE_AI_TALK(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global process_function,txt_entry
			        txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			        txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'我提出的问题: {process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]}\n')
			        PluginB.update()
			        txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			        try:
			            import invokeAI_LvfanAI
			            word=process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]
			            answer=invokeAI_LvfanAI.search(word, txt_entry, process_function, process_b_id, i, j)
			            pd=list(answer)
			            if pd[0]=='发' and pd[1]=='生' and pd[2]=='错' and pd[3]==' 误':
			                txt_entry.tag_config('error', foreground='#FF6A6A')
			                txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'{answer}\n','error')
			                PlunB_stop()
			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			            txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'{answer}\n')
			            txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			            PluginB.update()
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i, j, e)
			            PlunB_stop()
			    def DEPLOYMENT_AI(process_b_id_i_j,i_i,j_j):
			        global process_function, txt_entry,click_check_yn,click_id_i_t,j
			        click_check_yn=True
			        try:
			
			            place=f'{process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][1]}'
			            version=f'{process_function[int(process_b_id_i_j)][2]}'
			            import invokeAI_LvfanAI
			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			            answer=invokeAI_LvfanAI.deployment(place,version,i_i,j_j,process_b_id_i_j,process_function,process_b_id)
			            pd=list(answer)
			            if pd[0]=='发' and pd[1]=='生' and pd[2]=='错' and pd[3]=='误':
			                txt_entry.tag_config('error', foreground='#FF6A6A')
			                txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'{answer}\n','error')
			                PlunB_stop()
			            txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'{answer}\n')
			            PluginB.update()
			            txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i_i, j_j, e)
			            PlunB_stop()
			           
			        finally:
			            j+=1
			            click_check_yn=False
			            #print('*******************************')
			            PlunB_running(click_id_i_t)
			    def INVOKE_AI_TALK_start(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global click_check_yn
			        click_check_yn=True
			        PluginB.after(0,INVOKE_AI_TALK(process_b_id_i_j,i,j))
			    def DEPLOYMENT_AI_start(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        global click_check_yn
			        click_check_yn=True
			        PluginB.after(0,DEPLOYMENT_AI(process_b_id_i_j,i,j))
			    def scrolled(process_b_id_i_j,i,j):
			        try:
			            global txt_entry
			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			            txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'尝试关闭AI\n')
			            PluginB.update()
			            txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			            import invokeAI_LvfanAI
			            invokeAI_LvfanAI.DESTROY
			        except Exception as e:
			            ERROR(i, j, e)
			    c=0
			    i_j=[]
			    run_start=False
			    running_yn=True
			    a=-1
			    item_start=True
			    def use():
			        global click_check_yn, i_j,running_yn,run_start,j,c,txt_entry,item_start
			        global a
			        #print(f'click_check_yn:{click_check_yn}   a:{a}    running_yn:{running_yn} run_start:{run_start}  item_start:{item_start}')
			        if item_start==False:return
			        elif a==len(i_j)-1 and run_start==True:
			            #print(f'a:{a}')
			            PlunB_stop()
			            return
			        elif (click_check_yn==False or click_check_yn==None) and running_yn==True and item_start==True:
			            run_start=False
			            try:
			                 c += 1
			                 s=None
			                 for q in process_b_id:
			                     if int (q)!=c-1:continue
			                     for i in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                         #print(process_b_id[q][i])
			                         if process_b_id[q][i]!=None:
			                             s=1
			                 if s==1:
			                     txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                     txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'\n执行第{c}项\n')
			                     PluginB.update()
			                     txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                 
			                 a+=1
			                 #print(f'--------------------i:{a}')
			                 PlunB_running(i_j[a])
			                 
			            except:
							pass
			                #print('use pass')
			    def PlunB_run():
			        global item_start,a,run_start,txt_entry,process, process_b_id, process_button, process_function, click_check_yn,c,i_j,running_yn
			        #print(f'start')
			        txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			        txt_entry.delete('1.0', tk.END)
			        count = 0
			        for i in process_b_id:
			            for q in range(len(process_b_id[i])):
			                count += 1
			        txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'插件块运行共:{len(process_b_id)}项 , 共:{count}块，等待0.5秒执行命令\n')
			        PluginB.update()
			        txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			        c = 0
			        b = 0
			        for i in process_b_id:
			            for z in range(len(process_b_id[i])):
			                if (process_b_id[i][z] != None):
			                    b = 1
			        if b != 1: return
			        b = 0
			        #提取所有项名
			        #print(process_b_id)
			        for q in process_b_id:
			           i_j.append(q)
			        #print(i_j)
			        a=-1
			        #run_start=True
			        item_start=True
			        use()
			    def PlunB_running(i):
			            global click_check_yn_t,click_id_i_t,process,process_b_id,txt_entry,process_button,process_function,click_check_yn,click_id_i,j,c,run_start,running_yn
			            if click_check_yn == True or item_start==False or click_check_yn_t == True :
			                #print(f'click_check_yn:{click_check_yn}   run_start:{run_start}')
			                #print(f'return')
			                return
			            #开始运行
			            if running_yn==True:
			                file_menu3.entryconfig(0,state='disabled')
			                file_menu3.entryconfig(2,state='normal')
			            #print(f'###########################\nj:{j}   i:{i}')
			            if j>len(process_b_id[i])-1:
			                #print('0')
			                run_start = True
			                running_yn=True
			                j=0
			                #print(f'j return')
			                use()
			                
			            else:
			                run_start ,running_yn= False,False
			                try:
			                    #print(f'click_check:{click_check_yn}')
			                    #print(f'process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] :{process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]}')
			                    if process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] ==None:
			                        j+=1
			                        return
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '生成标签':
			                        make_text(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)#,防止被检测成int而报错
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='移动鼠标':
			                        move_mouse(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='输入文本':
			                        text_insert(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='点击鼠标左键':
			                        click_left(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='点击鼠标右键':
			                        click_right(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='粘贴':
			                        CTR_V(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='复制':
			                        CTR_C(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='剪切':
			                        CTR_X(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='拖动鼠标到':
			                        long_left_mouse(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='等待x秒':
			                         wait_minute(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                         j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='删除标签':
			                         delete_r(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                         j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='按压键盘单键':
			                         click_long(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                         j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='释放键盘单键':
			                         click_relax(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                         j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='滚动鼠标滚轮':
			                        scrolled(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='当按下x键时':
			                         txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                         txt_entry.insert(tk.END, f'监听键盘中,直至出现 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]} ...\n')
			                         txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                         PluginB.update()
			                         click_check_yn = True
			                         click_id_i = i
			                         click_check(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        
			                         j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '当x：x时':
			                         txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                         txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'时间监测中,直至出现 {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][1]} : {process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][2]}...\n')
			                         txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                         PluginB.update()
			                         #print('------------------------------------------------------------')
			                         click_check_yn_t = True
			                         click_id_i_t = i
			                         time_check_wait(int(process_b_id[i][j]), i, j)
			                         
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0]=='AI初始化':
			                        txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			                        txt_entry.insert(tk.END, '准备初始化AI进程...\n')
			                        PluginB.update()
			                        txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			                        click_check_yn=True
			                        click_id_i_t = i
			                        DEPLOYMENT_AI_start(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                        
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI回答' or process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI搜索' or process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI翻译' or process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI写作' or process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI生图' or process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '调用AI编程':
			                        INVOKE_AI_TALK_start(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                    elif process_function[int(process_b_id[i][j])][0] == '关闭AI':
			                        INVOKE_AI_CLOSE(int(process_b_id[i][j]),i,j)
			                        j+=1
			                except:
			                    j+=1
			                    pass
			                finally:
			                 
			                    running_yn = True
			                    txt_entry.see(tk.END)
			                PluginB.after(0,PlunB_running(i))
			    def PlunB_control():
			        global run_start,j,i_j,click_check_yn,running_yn,item_start
			        item_start=False
			        #print(f'stop  j:{j} ')
			        j=0
			        a=0
			        i_j=[]
			        run_start = False
			        running_yn=True
			        click_check_yn=None
			    def PlunB_stop():
			        global txt_entry
			        PlunB_control()
			        file_menu3.entryconfig(0, state='normal')
			        file_menu3.entryconfig(2, state='disabled')
			        txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			
			        txt_entry.insert(tk.END, '☑ 结束进程\n')
			        txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			
			    def PlunB_continue():
			        global txt_entry
			        PlunB_control()
			        PlunB_run()
			
			    file_menu2.add_separator()
			    file_menu2.add_command(label="模版",state='disabled', command=exchange)
			
			    # 修复后的代码行
			    file_menu3.add_command(label='运行',command=PlunB_run)                             # 执行PlunB_run函数
			    file_menu3.add_command(label="停止", command=PlunB_stop)
			    file_menu3.add_command(label="重启",state='disabled', command=PlunB_continue)
			
			    file_menu4.add_command(label="介绍", command=exchange)
			
			    menu_bar.add_cascade(label='文件',menu=file_menu)
			    menu_bar.add_cascade(label='编辑',menu=file_menu2)
			    menu_bar.add_cascade(label='控制',menu=file_menu3)
			    menu_bar.add_cascade(label='关于',menu=file_menu4)
			    #设置菜单栏到窗口
			    PluginB.config(menu=menu_bar)
			
			    count = 0
			    btn_p_x=0
			    btn_p_y=0
			    start=True
			    count_again=0
			    team=0
			    # 修复后的按钮校准功能代码
			    # 修复了闭包陷阱、事件绑定和校准逻辑问题
			    process_button={}
			    process_b_id={}
			    process=0
			    process_b_id_num=0
			    process_function={}

			    text_frame_List=[]

			    btn_team=[]

			    _global_image_cache = []
