			    img_edge=None
			    def cout_make(title):
			        global stop_repeat_num,count, printff, button_id,process_button,process,process_b_id,team,btn_team,process_function,text_frame_num,text_frame_List,entry_control
			        global process_b_id_num,img_chrome,img_edge
			        if stop_repeat_num==0:return
			        stop_repeat_num=0
			        button_id += 1
			        current_id = button_id  # 创建当前ID的副本避免闭包陷阱
			        # 修复1：添加event参数以匹配bind调用约定
			        def start_repeat(event, btn_id=current_id):  # 增加event参数
			            """启动连续触发机制"""
			            global repeat_id, start
			            start = True
			            cout(btn_id)
			        def control_text_frame(btn_id):
			            global text_frame_num,text_frame_List,process_button,process_b_id
			            # 部署项目分割框
			            for i in range(len(text_frame_List)):  # 删除所有分割框
			                try:
			                    text_frame_List[i].destroy()
			                except:
			                    #print(f'control_text_frame_1 pass')
			                    pass
			            text_frame_List = []
			            #print(f'process_b_id: {process_b_id} process_button:{process_button}')
			            j=0
			            for i in process_b_id:  # 重新分割
			                # print('部署')
			                    close=0
			                # try:
			                    for z in range(len(process_b_id[i])):
			                        #print(f'process_button[int(process_b_id[i][z])]:{process_button[int(process_b_id[i][z])]}   i:{i} z:{z}')
			                        try:
			                            a=process_button[int(process_b_id[i][z])]
			                        except:
			                            continue
			                        else:
			                            #print(f'j:{j}')
			                            text_frame = tk.Label(right_frame, text=f'第{j + 1}个项目', bg=right_frame_color)
			                            text_frame_List.append(text_frame)  # bg=root.cget("bg")匹配窗口背景颜色
			                            text_frame_List[j].place(anchor=tk.S, x=process_button[int(process_b_id[i][z])][0] + 40,
			                                                     y=process_button[int(process_b_id[i][z])][1] - 10, )  # anchor=tk.S放在底部(place)
			                            close=1
			                            break
			                    if close==0: j-=1
			                    j+=1
			
			        def PROCESS(btn_id):
			            global right_frame_color,start, btn_p_x, btn_p_y, count_again, process_button, process, process_b_id, team, btn_team, process_b_id_num, text_frame_num, text_frame_List
			            if len(process_b_id) == 0:   #当为第一块插件块生成时
			                #字典添加
			                process_b_id.update({0:[str(btn_id)]})
			                process_button.update({0:[btn_p_x,btn_p_y]})
			                #字典-列表添加
			                #process_b_id[0].append(button_id)
			            else:
			                add_btn=0
			                #print(f'btn_p_x:{btn_p_x}  btn_p_y:{btn_p_y}')
			                add_continue=0
			                for i in button_place:
			                   try:
			                        #print(f'i:{i}')
			                        #print(f'button_place{button_place}')
			                        #查找是否有跟id:i的btn为一组的
			                        if (int(button_place[i][0])==int(btn_p_x) and int(button_place[i][1])+58==int(btn_p_y)) or (int(button_place[i][0])==int(btn_p_x) and int(button_place[i][1])-58==int(btn_p_y)):
			                            if add_continue==1: #如果查找到第二次(带有了标记)
			                                continue  #直接返回
			                            add_continue=1 #如果查找到第一次则标记
			                            #查找到有跟id:i的btn为一组的
			                            #print('have btn\n')
			                            add_btn = 1
			                            repeat_id=None
			                            repeat_p=None
			                            for q in process_b_id:
			                                for j in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                                    #print(f'j:{j}')
			                                    try:
			                                        if int(process_b_id[q][int(j)]) == int(btn_id):   #循环查找是否曾今在process_id中记录过
			                                            #如果记录过则
			                                            repeat_p=q #标记repeat_p为记录过的项
			                                            repeat_id=j#标记repeat_id为记录过项的编号
			                                            break
			                                    except:
			                                        #print(f'process_2 pass')
			                                        continue
			                            # 如果未查找到且没在process_id中记录过
			                            #print(f'process_button[int(btn_id)][0]:{process_button[int(btn_id)][0]}   [1]:{process_button[int(btn_id)][1]}    \nbutton_place:{button_place[btn_id][0]}    {button_place[btn_id][1]}')
			                            if repeat_id==None and repeat_p==None:
			                                #print("insert btn's project\n")
			                                #插入到对应项目中
			                                for q in process_b_id:
			                                    for j in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                                        try:
			                                            #循环查找process_b_id的第q项,编号为j的btn的place_y+50为当前btn_y
			                                            if int(process_button[int(process_b_id[q][j])][1])+58 == int(button_place[btn_id][1]):
			                                                #只需匹配一次即可
			                                                process_b_id[q].insert(j+1,str(btn_id))#在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j+1插入btn_id
			                                                process_button.update({btn_id:[btn_p_x,btn_p_y]})#在process_button中记录该btn当前记录到process_b_id时的place
			                                                break
			                                            if int(process_button[int(process_b_id[q][j])][1])-58 == int(button_place[btn_id][1]):
			                                                #只需匹配一次即可
			                                                if j>0:
			                                                    process_b_id[q].insert(j-1,str(btn_id))#在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j-1插入btn_id
			                                                else:
			                                                    process_b_id[q].insert(0, str(btn_id))  # 在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j-1插入btn_id
			
			                                                process_button.update({btn_id:[btn_p_x,btn_p_y]})#在process_button中记录该btn当前记录到process_b_id时的place
			                                                break
			                                        except:
			                                            #print(f'process_3 pass')
			                                            pass
			                            #否则如果在process_id中记录过，检测其当前的process_button_x && _y是否与现在的button_place_x && _y相同
			                            elif process_button[int(btn_id)][0] == button_place[int(btn_id)][0] and process_button[int(btn_id)][1] == button_place[int(btn_id)][1]:
			                                #如果相同则通过无进程
			                                #print(f'no running\n')
			                                pass
			                            #否则如果在process_id中记录过，检测其当前的process_button_place与现在的button_place不同
			                            else:
			                                #调换process_b_id && 更新process_b_button
			                                #print("change btn's process_b_id && process_button\n")
			                                #print(f'len(process_b_id) = {len(process_b_id)}')
			                                exchange_id=None
			                                process_button[int(btn_id)][0] = btn_p_x
			                                process_button[int(btn_id)][1] = btn_p_y
			                                for z in range(len(process_b_id[repeat_p])):
			                                    try:
			                                        #print(f'循环一次')
			                                        #循环检测button_place_y第(process_b_id第repeat_p'重复的项'的编号为z)的项+50与当前button_place_y第btn_id的项是否相同
			                                        #print(f'button_place[int(process_b_id[repeat_p][z])][1]:{int(button_place[int(process_b_id[repeat_p][z])][1])}   button_place[int(btn_id)[1]:{button_place[int(btn_id)][1]}')
			                                        #print(f'repeat_p:{repeat_p}  z:{z}   process_b_id[repeat_p][z]:{process_b_id[repeat_p][z]}   btn_id:{btn_id}')
			                                        if int(process_b_id[repeat_p][z])==btn_id:
			                                            #print('continue')
			                                            continue
			                                        if button_place[int(process_b_id[repeat_p][z])][1]+58 == button_place[int(btn_id)][1]:
			                                            #print(f'记录exchange_id')
			                                            exchange_id=z#相同则记exchange_id'交换的位置id'为(第process_b_idd第repeat_p'重复的项'的编号为z)
			                                            break
			                                        # 循环检测button_place_y第(process_b_id第repeat_p'重复的项'的编号为z)的项-50与当前button_place_y第btn_id的项是否相同
			                                        if button_place[int(process_b_id[repeat_p][z])][1]-58 == button_place[int(btn_id)][1]:
			                                            #print(f'记录exchange_id')
			                                            exchange_id=z#相同则记exchange_id'交换的位置id'为(第process_b_idd第repeat_p'重复的项'的编号为z)
			                                            break
			                                    except:
			                                        #print(f'process_4 pass')
			                                        pass
			
			
			                                #print(f'repeat_id:{repeat_id}   exchange_id:{exchange_id}')
			                                if exchange_id==None:#要交换的btn和当前的btn不在同一个项中
			
			                                    for j in range(len(process_b_id[repeat_p])):
			                                       try:
			                                            #循环查找重复的项的id
			                                            if int(process_b_id[repeat_p][j])==int(btn_id):
			                                                to_delete=j
			                                                break
			                                       except:
			                                           #print(f'process_5 pass')
			                                           pass
			                                    #删除重复的项的id
			                                    try:
			                                        process_b_id[repeat_p].pop(to_delete)
			                                        if len(process_b_id[repeat_p])==0:process_b_id.pop(repeat_p)
			                                    except:
			                                        pass
			                                    for q in process_b_id:
			                                        for j in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                                            try:
			                                                # 循环查找process_b_id的第q项,编号为j的btn的place_y+50为当前btn_y
			                                                if int(process_button[int(process_b_id[q][j])][1]) + 58 == int(button_place[btn_id][1]):
			                                                    # 只需匹配一次即可
			                                                    process_b_id[q].insert(j + 1, str(btn_id))  # 在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j+1插入btn_id
			                                                    process_button.update({btn_id: [btn_p_x,  btn_p_y]})  # 在process_button中记录该btn当前记录到process_b_id时的place
			                                                    break
			                                                if int(process_button[int(process_b_id[q][j])][1]) - 58 == int(button_place[btn_id][1]):
			                                                    # 只需匹配一次即可
			                                                    if j > 0:
			                                                        process_b_id[q].insert(j - 1,   str(btn_id))  # 在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j-1插入btn_id
			                                                    else:
			                                                        process_b_id[q].insert(0, str(btn_id))  # 在process_b_id的第q项的编号为j-1插入btn_id
			
			                                                    process_button.update({btn_id: [btn_p_x,btn_p_y]})  # 在process_button中记录该btn当前记录到process_b_id时的place
			                                                    break
			                                            except:
			                                                pass
			                                elif repeat_idexchange_id:#重复的项在要交换的编号后面
			                                    for p in range(repeat_id-1,exchange_id-1,-1):
			                                        try:
			                                         process_b_id[repeat_p][p+1]=str(process_b_id[repeat_p][p])
			                                        except:
			                                            pass
			                                    try:
			                                     process_b_id[repeat_p][exchange_id]=str(btn_id)
			                                    except:
			                                        pass
			                   except:
			                        #print(f'process_1 pass')
			                        continue
			                if add_btn==0: #未检测到且没有btn能与当前的btn搭配
			                    #print('add btn\n')
			                    to_delete=None
			                    for q in process_b_id:  # 获取键的快照，避免迭代时被修改
			                        for j in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                            try:
			                                #循环检测之前有没有被记录过
			                                if int(process_b_id[q][j]) == int(btn_id):
			                                    #如果被记录过则删去
			                                    process_button.pop(int(btn_id))
			                                    process_b_id[q].pop(j)
			                                    if(len(process_b_id[q])==0):
			                                        #如果process_b_id的项为空则删去process_b_id的项
			                                        to_delete=q
			                                        break
			                                    break
			                            except:
			                                pass
			                    if to_delete == None:
			                        # 新建项目和编号
			                        process_b_id_num += 1
			                        process_b_id.update({process_b_id_num: [str(btn_id)]})
			                    else:
			                        # 在空项插入
			                        process_b_id[to_delete] = [str(btn_id)]
			                    process_button.update({int(btn_id): [btn_p_x, btn_p_y]})
			            # 调试输出
			            #print(f'process_button:{process_button}')
			            #print(f'process_b_id:{process_b_id}\n-----------------\n')
			
			            control_text_frame(btn_id)
			        def stop_repeat(event, btn_id=current_id):
			            global change_yn,stop_repeat_num,start, btn_p_x, btn_p_y, count_again,process_button,process,process_b_id,team,btn_team,process_b_id_num,text_frame_num,text_frame_List
			            stop_repeat_num=1
			            change_yn = False
			            start = False
			            # 获取理想落点（来自 cout 最后一次更新）
			            ideal_x = int(btn_p_x)
			            ideal_y = int(btn_p_y)
			            #print(f'btn_p_x:{btn_p_x}   btn_p_y:{btn_p_y}\n-------\n')
			            # 先把所有按钮坐标转为整数（包括自己）
			            for i in button_place:
			                try:
			                    button_place[i][0] = int(button_place[i][0])
			                    button_place[i][1] = int(button_place[i][1])
			                except:
			                    #print(f'stop_repeat_1 pass')
			                    pass
			            # 向下避让：直到当前位置不与任何其他按钮重叠
			            final_x, final_y = ideal_x, ideal_y
			            while True:
			                overlap = False
			                for i in range(len(button_place)):
			                    try:
			                        if i == btn_id:
			                            continue
			                        ox, oy = button_place[i][0], button_place[i][1]
			                        # 判断是否重叠：水平接近（±60）且垂直接近（±15）
			                        if abs(final_x - ox) <= 65 and abs(final_y - oy) <= 15:
			                            overlap = True
			                            final_x= ox
			                            final_y =oy+ 58  # 向下偏移
			                            break  # 重新检查所有按钮
			                    except:
			                        pass
			                if not overlap:
			                    break
			            # 更新当前按钮位置
			            button_place[btn_id][0] = final_x
			            button_place[btn_id][1] = final_y
			            printff[btn_id].place(x=final_x, y=final_y)
			
			            #print(f'按钮放置：{final_x}  {final_y}')
			            #print(f'button_place:{button_place}')
			            # 清除提示标签
			            label_remind.place_forget()
			            PROCESS(int(btn_id))
			
			        def cout(btn_id):
			            global printff, button_place, start, btn_p_x, btn_p_y,change_yn
			            if start != True:
			                return
			            change_yn = True
			            screen_x, screen_y = pyautogui.position()
			            container_x = screen_x - right_frame.winfo_rootx()-10
			            container_y = screen_y - right_frame.winfo_rooty()-10
			            button_place[btn_id][0] = int(container_x)
			            button_place[btn_id][1] = int(container_y)
			            printff[btn_id].place(x=container_x, y=container_y)
			            #printff[btn_id].config(cursor="heart")  # 点击后切换为心形光标
			            remind = 0
			            # 匹配校准remind_label
			            remind_p_min=0x3f
			            remind_p_id=0
			            for i in button_place:
			                try:
			                    button_place[i][0] = int(button_place[i][0])
			                    button_place[i][1] = int(button_place[i][1])
			                    button_place[btn_id][0] = int(button_place[btn_id][0])
			                    button_place[btn_id][1] = int(button_place[btn_id][1])
			                    if i == int(btn_id):
			                        continue
			                    if (button_place[i][0] - 105 <= button_place[btn_id][0] and button_place[i][0] + 105 >= button_place[btn_id][0]):
			                        if (button_place[i][1] - 145 <= button_place[btn_id][1] and button_place[i][1] + 145 >= button_place[btn_id][1]):
			                            remind_min=remind_p_min
			                            if(button_place[i][1]-button_place[btn_id][1]>0):
			                                remind_p_min=min(remind_p_min,button_place[i][1]-button_place[btn_id][1])
			                            else:
			                                remind_p_min=min(remind_p_min,button_place[btn_id][1]-button_place[i][1])
			
			                            if(remind_p_min!=remind_min): remind_p_id=i
			                            remind += 1
			                except:
			                    pass
			            if remind == 0:
			                try:
			                    btn_p_x = button_place[btn_id][0]
			                    btn_p_y = button_place[btn_id][1]
			                    label_remind.place_forget()
			                except:
			                    pass
			            else:
			                try:
			                    if button_place[remind_p_id][1] < button_place[btn_id][1]:
			                        btn_p_y = button_place[remind_p_id][1] + 58
			                    else:
			                        btn_p_y = button_place[remind_p_id][1] - 58
			                    btn_p_x = button_place[remind_p_id][0]
			                    label_remind.config(text='                           \n                          ', bg='#D4D4D4')
			                    label_remind.place(x=btn_p_x, y=btn_p_y)
			                    #print(f'移动:{btn_p_x,btn_p_y}')
			                except:
			                    pass
			            repeat_id = PluginB.after(50, lambda: cout(btn_id))  # 使用lambda传递参数
			
			
			        def delete_btn(btn_id):
			            global printff,process_button,button_place,process_b_id,process_function,text_frame_num,text_frame_List
			            try:
			                printff[btn_id].destroy()
			                printff[btn_id]=None
			                process_function[btn_id] = [None]
			                process_button[btn_id]=None
			                button_place[btn_id]=None
			                to_delete, to_delete_x = None, None
			                for q in process_b_id:
			                    for j in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                        try:
			                            if (int(process_b_id[q][j]) == int(btn_id)):
			                                to_delete, to_delete_x = j, q
			                        except:
			                            pass
			                if to_delete != None and to_delete_x != None:
			                    process_b_id[to_delete_x][to_delete]=None
			
			                # 部署项目分割框
			                control_text_frame(btn_id)
			            except:
			                pass
			        def change_name(btn_id,button_id):
			            global process_function,_global_image_cache
			            INSERT=tk.Tk()
			            INSERT.title('插件块自定义')
			            INSERT.resizable(False, False)
			            INSERT.geometry('348x220')
			            INSERT.attributes('-topmost', True)
			
			            #配置entry设置
			            label = tk.Label(INSERT,font=('微软雅黑 Light',10,'bold'))
			            label.place(x=28, y=30)
			
			            def ok():
			                global process_function
			                nonlocal button_id,mouse_x_s,mouse_y_s,mouse_x_e,mouse_y_e,mouse_y_e
			                if process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '生成标签' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '输入文本':
			                    if entry_control.get()=='':return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1]=entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '移动鼠标':
			                    if mouse_x_s and mouse_y_s == None: return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1]=mouse_x_s
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][2]=mouse_y_s
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: x: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]}   y:{process_function[int(btn_id)][2]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='点击鼠标左键' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='点击鼠标右键':
			                    if entry_control.get()=='':return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1]=entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} 秒')
			                elif  process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='滚动鼠标滚轮' :
			                    if entry_control.get()=='':return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1]=entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} 个单位')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '调用AI生图' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI写作' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI翻译' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI搜索' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI编程' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI回答':
			                    if entry_control.get()=='':return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1]=entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: 运行内容:{process_function[int(btn_id)][1]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '当按下x键时'  :
			                    if entry_control.get() == '': return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(
			                        text=f'当按下 {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} 时')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '按压键盘单键' :
			                    if entry_control.get() == '': return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(
			                        text=f'按压键盘单件: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '释放键盘单键':
			                    if entry_control.get() == '': return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(
			                            text=f'释放键盘单件: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '当x：x时' :
			                    if entry_control.get() == '': return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][2] = entry_control2.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(
			                        text=f'当 {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} : {process_function[int(btn_id)][2]} 时')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '等待x秒':
			                    if entry_control.get() == '': return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(
			                        text=f'等待 {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} 秒')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '拖动鼠标到':
			                    #print(f'{mouse_x_s}  {mouse_y_s}  {mouse_x_e}  {mouse_y_e}')
			                    if mouse_x_s==None or mouse_y_s==None or mouse_x_e ==None or mouse_y_e== None: return
			                    #print(1)
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = mouse_x_s
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][2] = mouse_y_s
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][3] = mouse_x_e
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][4] = mouse_y_e
			
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}: 起始位置x: {process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} y:{process_function[int(btn_id)][2]}   结束位置:x: {process_function[int(btn_id)][3]} y:{process_function[int(btn_id)][4]}')
			                elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == 'AI初始化':
			                    if entry_control.get() == '' or entry_control2.get()=='' or VERSION==None: return
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][1] = entry_control.get()
			                    process_function[int(btn_id)][2] = entry_control2.get()
			                    printff[int(button_id)].configure(text=f'初始化AI {VERSION}地址:{process_function[int(btn_id)][1]} ,版本号:{process_function[int(btn_id)][2]}')
			                    btn_ok.place(x=30,y=140,height=36,width=134)
			                    btn_cancel.place(x=180,y=140,height=36,width=134)
			                #print(f'process_function:{process_function}')
			                INSERT.destroy()
			            def cancel():
			                nonlocal INSERT
			                try:
			                    INSERT.destroy()
			                finally:
			                    pass
			            btn_ok=ttk.Button(INSERT,style='TButton',text='确定',command=ok)
			            btn_cancel=ttk.Button(INSERT,style='TButton',text='取消',command=cancel)
			            btn_ok.place(x=30,y=140,height=36,width=134)
			            btn_cancel.place(x=180,y=140,height=36,width=134)
			            PluginB.bind('', lambda event: ok())
			
			
			
			            mouse_x_s, mouse_y_s,mouse_x_e,mouse_y_e ,VERSION= None, None,None,None,None
			            if process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='生成标签' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='输入文本' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '调用AI生图' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI写作' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI翻译' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI搜索' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI编程' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='调用AI回答':
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 运行内容设为' )
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=80,height=36,width=285)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='移动鼠标':
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 移动坐标设为')
			                label.place(x=28,y=15)
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT,style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=96,height=36,width=285)
			                def move():
			
			                    label_r=tk.Label(INSERT,text='鼠标点击停止',font=('微软雅黑 Light',9,'bold'))
			                    label_r.place(x=180,y=53)
			
			                    def update_entry(x, y):
			                        """
			                        主线程执行的界面更新函数
			                        所有Tkinter组件操作都放在这里
			                        """
			                        entry_control.configure(state=tk.NORMAL)
			                        entry_control.delete(0, tk.END)
			                        entry_control.insert(tk.END, f'x: {x}     y: {y}\n')
			              
			                    def on_click(x,y,button_,pressed):
			                        nonlocal mouse_x_s,mouse_y_s
			                        mouse_x_s=x
			                        mouse_y_s=y
			                        move.listener.stop()  # 停止监听器
			                        PluginB.after(0, lambda: update_entry(mouse_x_s, mouse_y_s))
			                        return False  # 关键：返回False终止监听器
			                        # 存储监听器引用
			
			                    move.listener = mouse.Listener(on_click=on_click)
			                    move.listener.start()
			
			                btn_move_record = ttk.Button(INSERT, style='TButton', text='一键录入', command=move)
			                btn_move_record.place(x=30, y=53, height=36, width=134)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '点击鼠标左键' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='点击鼠标右键' or  process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='等待x秒':
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 运行时间设为(秒)')
			                label.place(x=13,y=30)
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END,'1')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=80,height=36,width=285)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='滚动鼠标滚轮' :
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 运行长度设为(单位)')
			                label.place(x=0,y=30)
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END,'1')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=80,height=36,width=285)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '按压键盘单键' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='当按下x键时' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='释放键盘单键':
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 按键设为(秒)')
			                label.place(x=28,y=30)
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END,'A,Shift,Control,1')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=80,height=36,width=285)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '当x：x时':
			                #print(1)
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 时间设为')
			                label.place(x=28,y=30)
			                entry_control=ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                hour = datetime.now().strftime("%H")
			                minute = datetime.now().strftime("%M")
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END,f'{hour}')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control.place(x=30,y=80,height=36,width=130)
			                label2=tk.Label(INSERT,text=':')
			                label2.place(x=165,y=80)
			                entry_control2 = ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control2.insert(tk.END, f'{minute}')
			                entry_control2.bind('', lambda e: entry_control2.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control2.place(x=185, y=80, height=36, width=130)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0] == '拖动鼠标到':
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 移动坐标设为')
			                label.place(x=28, y=15)
			                entry_control = ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.place(x=30, y=96, height=36, width=136)
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END, '起始位置')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control2 = ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control2.place(x=180, y=96, height=36, width=136)
			                entry_control2.insert(tk.END, '终止位置')
			                entry_control2.bind('', lambda e: entry_control2.delete(0, tk.END))
			
			                cout=0
			                def move():
			                    nonlocal cout
			                    cout+=1
			                    if cout>2:
			                        move.listener.stop()  # 停止监听器
			                        return False  # 关键：返回False终止监听器
			                    label_r = tk.Label(INSERT, text='鼠标点击停止', font=('微软雅黑 Light', 9, 'bold'))
			                    label_r.place(x=180, y=53)
			                    def update_entry(x, y):
			                        nonlocal cout
			                        """
			                        主线程执行的界面更新函数
			                        所有Tkinter组件操作都放在这里
			                        """
			                        if cout==1:
			                            entry_control.configure(state=tk.NORMAL)
			                            entry_control.delete(0, tk.END)
			                            entry_control.insert(tk.END, f'x: {x}     y: {y}\n')
			                       
			                        elif cout==2:
			                            entry_control2.configure(state=tk.NORMAL)
			                            entry_control2.delete(0, tk.END)
			                            entry_control2.insert(tk.END, f'x: {x}     y: {y}\n')
			                        
			
			                    def on_click(x, y, button_, pressed):
			                        nonlocal mouse_x_s, mouse_y_s,mouse_x_e,mouse_y_e,cout
			                        if cout==1:
			                            mouse_x_s = x
			                            mouse_y_s = y
			                            PluginB.after(0, lambda: update_entry(mouse_x_s, mouse_y_s))
			                        elif cout==2:
			                            mouse_x_e = x
			                            mouse_y_e = y
			                            PluginB.after(0, lambda: update_entry(mouse_x_e, mouse_y_e))
			
			                        move.listener.stop()  # 停止监听器
			                        return False  # 关键：返回False终止监听器
			
			                    move.listener = mouse.Listener(on_click=on_click)
			                    move.listener.start()
			
			
			                btn_move_record = ttk.Button(INSERT, style='TButton', text='一键录入', command=move)
			                btn_move_record.place(x=30, y=53, height=36, width=134)
			            elif process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='AI初始化':
			                btn_ok.place(x=30,y=155)
			                btn_cancel.place(x=180,y=155)
			                label.config(text=f'将插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 运行浏览器设为')
			                label.place(x=28, y=11)
			                label2=tk.Label(INSERT, text='自定义设置')
			                label2.place(x=28, y=99)
			                entry_control = ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control.place(x=30, y=120, height=36, width=132)
			                entry_control.insert(tk.END,f'浏览器地址')
			                entry_control.bind('', lambda e: entry_control.delete(0, tk.END))
			                entry_control2 = ttk.Entry(INSERT, style='btn.TButton')
			                entry_control2.place(x=182, y=120, height=36, width=132)
			                entry_control2.insert(tk.END,f'版本号')
			                entry_control2.bind('', lambda e: entry_control2.delete(0, tk.END))
			
			                # full_image_path_chrome = 'Chrome图标.png'
			                # # 使用Pillow加载图片并调整大小（如果需要）
			                # original_image = Image.open(full_image_path_chrome)
			                # resized_image = original_image.resize((15, 15), Image.Resampling.LANCZOS)  # 调整大小

			        def show_place(btn_id):
			            global process_b_id,process_function,button_place
			            txt_entry.config(state='normal')
			            for q in process_b_id:
			                for i in range(len(process_b_id[q])):
			                    try:
			                        if(int(process_b_id[q][i]) == int(btn_id)):
			                            item=q
			                            num=i
			                    except:
			                        pass
			            try:
			                txt_entry.insert(tk.END,f'当前插件块 {process_function[int(btn_id)][0]} 信息:\n项目序: {item}    编号: {num}\n窗口位置: {button_place[int(btn_id)][0]} , {button_place[int(btn_id)][1]}\n\n')
			                txt_entry.config(state='disabled')
			            except:
			                pass

			            #print('ok')
			            try:
			                cout_make(process_function[int(btn_id)][0])
			            except:
			                pass
			
			        def show_menu(event,btn_id,button_id):
			            global process_function,menu_btn,change_yn
			            #显示右键菜单栏
			            if change_yn==True:return
			            menu_btn.entryconfig(0, command=lambda: delete_btn(btn_id))
			            menu_btn.entryconfig(2, command=lambda: copy_btn(btn_id))
			            #print(f'process_function[int(btn_id)][0]:{process_function[int(btn_id)][0]}')
			            if process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='剪切' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='粘贴' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='复制' or process_function[int(btn_id)][0]=='删除标签' :
			             menu_btn.entryconfig(1,state=tk.DISABLED)
			            else:
			                menu_btn.entryconfig(1,state=tk.NORMAL,command=lambda:change_name(btn_id,button_id))
			            menu_btn.entryconfig(4, command=lambda: show_place(btn_id))
			            menu_btn.post(event.x_root, event.y_root)  # y/x_root使用屏幕绝对坐标防止偏移,最后在弹出菜单
			            PluginB.bind('', lambda event: copy_btn(btn_id))

			            button_place.update({button_id: [50, 150]})  # 添加到字典

			            # 绑定事件（固定current_id值）
			            printff[button_id].bind("",lambda event, id=current_id: start_repeat(event, id))  # 显式传递ID
			            printff[button_id].bind("", lambda event, id=current_id: stop_repeat(event, id))
			            printff[button_id].bind("", lambda event,id=current_id,button_id=button_id: show_menu(event, id,button_id))  # 绑定右键
			
			            start_repeat(current_id)

			            # 用户资金
			            class Account:
			                def __init__(self, name, password, balance, operation, shenfen):
			                    self.name = name
			                    self.password = password
			                    self.balance = balance
			                    self.operation = operation
			                    self.shenfen = shenfen
			
			                def record(self):
			                    current_time = datetime.now()
			                    # 格式化时间字符串，年份只保留后两位
			                    current_time_str = f'{current_time.year % 100:02d}-{current_time.month:02d}-{current_time.day:02d}  {current_time.hour:02d}:{current_time.minute:02d}:{current_time.second:02d}'
			
			                    if (self.name != ''):
			                        f = open(self.name + ".rtf", "a")
			                        text = f"时间:{current_time}" + f"昵称:{self.name},密码:{self.password},当前资金:{self.balance},状态:{self.operation},身份:{self.shenfen}/&&\n"
			                        f.write(text)
			                        f.close()

			            class Account2:
			                def __init__(self, name, wupin, shoujia):
			                    self.name = name
			
			                    self.shoujia = shoujia
			                    self.wupin = wupin
			
			                def record_zhangben(self):
			                    current_time = datetime.now()
			                    # 格式化时间字符串，年份只保留后两位
			                    current_time_str = f'{current_time.year % 100:02d}-{current_time.month:02d}-{current_time.day:02d}  {current_time.hour:02d}:{current_time.minute:02d}:{current_time.second:02d}'
			
			                    if (self.name != ''):
			                        with open(self.name + "账本" + ".rtf", "a") as f:  # 使用with语句来确保文件正确关闭
			                            text = (
			                                f"时间:{current_time},昵称:{self.name},购买了售价:{self.shoujia},虚拟物品:{self.wupin}/&&\n")
			                            f.write(text)

			                    self.name = name

			                def record_history(self):
			                    current_time = datetime.now()
			                    # 格式化时间字符串，年份只保留后两位
			                    current_time_str = f'{current_time.year % 100:02d}-{current_time.month:02d}-{current_time.day:02d}  {current_time.hour:02d}:{current_time.minute:02d}:{current_time.second:02d}'
			
			                    if self.name != '':
			                        with open(self.name + "主控记录" + ".rtf", "a") as f:  # 使用with语句来确保文件正确关闭
			                            text = (
			                                f"时间:{current_time_str},昵称:{self.name}, 权限:{self.tongy}, 事件:{self.lishi},{self.caozuo}/&&\n")
			                            f.write(text)

			                    def 插入换行(文本):
			                        # 在每16个字符后插入一个换行符
			                        新文本 = ""
			                        for i in range(0, len(文本), 16):
			                            新文本 += 文本[i:i + 16] + "\n\n"
			                        return 新文本

			                def zhuxiao():
			                    def permanent_delete(file_path):
			                        """使用 Windows API 强制永久删除文件"""
			                        file_path = os.path.abspath(file_path)
			                        if not os.path.exists(file_path):
			                            return False
			                        try:
			                            class SHFILEOPSTRUCTW(ctypes.Structure):
			                                _fields_ = [
			                                    ("hwnd", ctypes.c_void_p),
			                                    ("wFunc", ctypes.c_uint),
			                                    ("pFrom", ctypes.c_wchar_p),
			                                    ("pTo", ctypes.c_wchar_p),
			                                    ("fFlags", ctypes.c_ushort),
			                                    ("fAnyOperationsAborted", ctypes.c_bool),
			                                    ("hNameMappings", ctypes.c_void_p),
			                                    ("lpszProgressTitle", ctypes.c_wchar_p),
			                                ]
			
			                            FO_DELETE = 0x0003
			                            FOF_SILENT = 0x0004
			                            FOF_NOCONFIRMATION = 0x0010
			                            FOF_NOERRORUI = 0x0400
			
			                            # 构造双NULL结尾的路径字符串
			                            pFrom = ctypes.create_unicode_buffer(file_path + '\0\0')
			
			                            fs = SHFILEOPSTRUCTW()
			                            fs.hwnd = 0
			                            fs.wFunc = FO_DELETE
			                            fs.pFrom = ctypes.cast(pFrom, ctypes.c_wchar_p)
			                            fs.pTo = None
			                            fs.fFlags = FOF_SILENT | FOF_NOCONFIRMATION | FOF_NOERRORUI
			                            fs.fAnyOperationsAborted = False
			                            fs.hNameMappings = 0
			                            fs.lpszProgressTitle = None
			
			                            result = ctypes.windll.shell32.SHFileOperationW(ctypes.byref(fs))
			                            return result == 0
			                        except Exception as e:
			                            print(f"永久删除失败: {e}")
			                            return False
			
			                    def delete_files():
			                        file_paths = file_listbox.get(0, tk.END)
			                        results = []
			                        for file_path in file_paths:
			                            file_path = file_path.strip()
			                            if not file_path:
			                                continue
			
			                            if os.path.exists(file_path):
			                                confirmed = messagebox.askyesno("确认删除", "删除文件后无法恢复！是否继续？")
			                                if confirmed:
			                                    try:
			                                        if permanent_delete(file_path):
			                                            results.append(f"文件 {file_path} 已永久删除.")
			                                        else:
			                                            results.append(f"删除失败: {file_path}")
			                                    except Exception as e:
			                                        results.append(f"删除错误 {file_path}: {str(e)}")
			                            else:
			                                results.append(f"文件不存在: {file_path}")
			
			                        result_text.delete('1.0', tk.END)
			                        result_text.insert(tk.END, '\n'.join(results))
			                        file_listbox.delete(0, tk.END)
			
			                    def choose_files():
			                        file_paths = filedialog.askopenfilenames()
			                        file_listbox.delete(0, tk.END)
			                        for path in file_paths:
			                            file_listbox.insert(tk.END, path)

			                                                        """检查指定的包是否已安装"""

			                                                        return spec is not None
			
			                                                    def install_package(package_name, qc):

			                        def install_and_import(package, package_name_for_install=None):
			                            """Install and import the given package if it's not already available."""
			                            package_name_for_install = package_name_for_install or package
			                            try:
			                                # Try to import the module
			                                importlib.import_module(package)
			                            except ImportError:
			                                response = messagebox.askyesno("缺少库", f"库 {package} 未安装。是否要现在安装？")
			                                if response:
			                                    try:
			                                        # Install the package using pip
			                                        subprocess.check_call(
			                                            [sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", package_name_for_install])
			                                        # messagebox.showinfo("安装完成", f"{package_name_for_install} 安装完成")
			                                        label_提 = tk.Label(qc, text=f"安装完成,{package_name_for_install} 安装完成",
			                                                            font=('微软雅黑', 8), bg='#bfffa9', fg='black')
			                                        label_提.place(x=78, y=9)
			                                        qc.after(2900, label_提.destroy)
			
			                                        # Import the module after installation
			                                        globals()[package] = importlib.import_module(package)
			                                    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
			                                        # messagebox.showerror("安装错误", f"安装 {package_name_for_install} 时发生错误: {e}")
			                                        label_提 = tk.Label(qc, text=f"安装错误,安装 {package_name_for_install} 时发生错误",
			                                                            font=('微软雅黑', 8), bg='#ffd4d4', fg='black')
			                                        label_提.place(x=70, y=9)
			                                        qc.after(3300, label_提.destroy)
			                                        sys.exit(
			                                            1)  # Exit program to prevent subsequent code from crashing due to missing library
			                                else:
			                                    # messagebox.showerror("手动安装", f"请手动安装 {package_name_for_install} 后再运行此程序。")
			                                    label_提 = tk.Label(qc,
			                                                        text=f"手动安装,请手动安装 {package_name_for_install} 后再运行此程序。",
			                                                        font=('微软雅黑', 8), bg='#ffd4d4', fg='black')
			                                    label_提.place(x=64, y=9)
			                                    qc.after(3600, label_提.destroy)
			                                    sys.exit(1)
			
			                        def ensure_libraries_installed():
			                            """Ensure all required libraries are installed."""
			                            required_libraries = {
			                                'cv2': 'opencv-python',
			                                'PIL': 'Pillow',  # 注意：导入时使用的是 from PIL import Image
			                                'PyPDF2': 'PyPDF2',
			                                'reportlab': 'reportlab'
			                            }
			                            for package, package_name_for_install in required_libraries.items():
			                                install_and_import(package, package_name_for_install)
			
			                        def show_message(title, message, msg_type='info'):
			                            """Display a message box with the given title and message."""
			                            if msg_type == 'info':
			                                messagebox.showinfo(title, message)
			                            elif msg_type == 'warning':
			                                messagebox.showwarning(title, message)
			                            elif msg_type == 'error':
			                                messagebox.showerror(title, message)

			                    def update_verification_code_display(code):
			                        canva = tk.Canvas(qc, width=100, height=34)
			                        canva.place(x=170, y=38, width=100, height=34)
			                        colours = ["red", "orange", "green", "yellow", "purple", "grey", "pink", "black"]
			                        theScreen = turtle.TurtleScreen(canva)
			                        asd = turtle.RawTurtle(theScreen)
			                        asd.penup()
			                        asd.goto(-30, -14)
			                        asd.pendown()
			                        asd.write(code, font=("Arial", 13, "normal"))
			                        asd.penup()
			                        asd.goto(-33, -7)
			                        asd.pendown()
			                        b = random.randint(0, 7)
			                        c = random.randint(8, 15)
			                        asd.color(colours[b])
			                        asd.write("-------------", font=("Arial", 11, "normal"))
			                        asd.penup()
			                        asd.goto(-33, -14)
			                        asd.pendown()
			                        asd.color(colours[c - 8])
			                        asd.write("————", font=("Arial", 11, "normal"))

			            def 便利贴OFFICE():
			                global PLUS_版本, 姓名, windows, txt_edit, tab_编号_助

			                word.geometry(f"520x495")
			                word.resizable(False, False)  # 禁止

			                def save_as():
			                    global 文本, PLUS_版本, tab_编号_助, 姓名, txt_edit, tab,txt_编号_助 
			                    nonlocal 旬报
			                    # 获取当前选项卡的索引 !
			                    current_tab_index = tabControl.index('current')
			                    # 获取用户保存的文件路径
			                    file_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(
			                        defaultextension=".json",
			                        filetypes=[("Text Files", "*.txt"), ("All Files", "*.*"), ("RTF Document", "*.rtf")]
			                    )
			
			                    if file_path:
			                        文本 = file_path
			                        save()  # 调用保存函数
			
			                    # 获取当前选项卡的文本内容
			                    旬报 = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].get('1.0', tk.END)
			                    # 提取文件名
			                    文本 = os.path.basename(文本)
			                    # 更改当前选项卡的文本
			                    if 文本 != "":
			                        tabControl.tab(current_tab_index, text=f"{文本}")
			
			                    # 记录操作日志
			                    uuser = Account1(姓名, '1', "另存标签文件:" + str(文本), "操作:10文件{重命名文件并定义格式}")
			                    uuser.record_history()
			
			                def save():
			                    global 文本, 旬报, 姓名, PLUS_版本, tab_编号_助, txt_edit,txt_编号_助
			                    name = 姓名
			                    if 文本 != "":
			                        try:
			                            # 获取文本内容
			                            content = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].get('1.0', tk.END).strip()
			                            # 获取文本格式信息
			                            format_info = []
			                            for tag in txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_names():
			                                ranges = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_ranges(tag)
			                                while ranges:
			                                    start = ranges[0]
			                                    end = ranges[1]
			                                    format_info.append({
			                                        "tag": tag,
			                                        "start": str(start),
			                                        "end": str(end),
			                                        "config": txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_cget(tag, "font"),
			                                        "color": txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_cget(tag, "foreground")
			                                    })
			                                    ranges = ranges[2:]
			
			                            # 创建一个包含文本内容和格式信息的字典
			                            data = {
			                                "content": content,
			                                "format_info": format_info
			                            }
			
			                            # 将数据保存到文件
			                            with open(文本, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file:
			                                json.dump(data, file, ensure_ascii=False, indent=4)
			                            旬报 = content
			                            文本 = os.path.basename(文本)
			                            # word.title( 文本 + f"-{PLUS_版本}")
			
			                            uuser = Account1(name, '1', "保存标签文件:" + str(文本), "操作:10文件{重命名文件/定义格式}")
			                            uuser.record_history()
			                        except Exception as e:
			                            tb = traceback.extract_tb(sys.exc_info()[2])
			                            error_message = f"{e} (line {tb[-1].lineno})"
			                            print(f"报错: {error_message}")
			                            messagebox.showerror(" 保存失败", f"保存文件时发生错误: {error_message}")
			                    else:
			                        save_as()

			                    def get_mouse_line(event=None):
			                        global tab_编号_助, tab, txt_编号_助
			                        global txt_edit
			                        # 获取鼠标位置对应的文本索引
			                        try:
			                            mouse_index = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(f"@{event.x},{event.y}")  # 解析出行号
			                            line_number = int(mouse_index.split('.')[0])
			                            line_label.config(text=f"Mouse: {line_number}")  # 更新标签显示当前行数
			                        except:
			                            mouse_index = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(f"@{event.x},{event.y}")
			                            # 解析出行号
			                            line_number = int(mouse_index.split('.')[0])
			                            # 更新标签显示当前行数
			                            line_label.config(text=f"Mouse: {line_number}")
			
			                    # 绑定鼠标移动事件
			                    txt_edit[txt_编号_助].bind("", get_mouse_line)
			                    # 创建标签用于显示鼠标所在的行数
			                    line_label = tk.Label(tab[tab_编号_助], text="Mouse:")
			                    line_label.place(x=307, y=447)
			
			                    # 检测光标所在行数
			                    def update_cursor_line(event=None):
			                        global tab_编号_助, txt_编号_助
			                        global txt_edit
			                        try:
			                            # 获取光标位置对应的文本索引
			                            cursor_index = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index("insert")
			                            # 解析出行号
			                            line_number = int(cursor_index.split('.')[0])
			                            # 更新标签显示当前光标所在行数
			                            line_label2.config(text=f"Ln: {line_number}")
			                        except:
			                            # 获取光标位置对应的文本索引
			                            cursor_index = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index("insert")
			                            # 解析出行号
			                            line_number = int(cursor_index.split('.')[0])
			                            # 更新标签显示当前光标所在行数
			                            line_label2.config(text=f"Ln: {line_number}")
			
			                    # 绑定事件以在光标移动时更新行数显示
			                    txt_edit[txt_编号_助].bind("", update_cursor_line)  # 键盘输入后更新
			                    txt_edit[txt_编号_助].bind("", update_cursor_line)  # 鼠标点击后更新
			                    # 初始化窗口状态
			                    last_state = word.wm_state()
			                    def on_configure(event):
			                        global tab, current_state, 频道, tab_编号_助, txt_edit, tab, txt_编号_助
			                        nonlocal last_state
			                        current_state = word.wm_state()
			                        if current_state != last_state:
			                            if current_state == 'zoomed':
			                                # 获取屏幕的宽度

			                                    txt_edit[txt_编号_助].config(width=int(screen_width / 7) - 48)  # 假设每个字符的平均宽度为7像素
			                                else:
			                                    return
			                            else:
			                                # 恢复默认宽度
			                                txt_edit[txt_编号_助].config(width=44)
			                            last_state = current_state
			                    # 绑定  事件
			                    word.bind('', on_configure)
			                    # 创建标签用于显示光标所在的行数
			                    line_label2 = tk.Label(tab[tab_编号_助], text="Ln: ")
			                    line_label2.place(x=7, y=447)

			                        """新建功能的函数"""

			                def 工作时间():

			                        return

			                def close():
			                    global 文本, a, 姓名, txt_edit, tab_编号_助, tab,txt_编号_助
			                    nonlocal 旬报, 工作时长, 工作判, 分, 秒, 时
			                    name = 姓名
			                    try:
			                        if 姓名 != "":
			                            # 当前工作时长
			                            时 = int(工作时长[0])
			                            分 = int(工作时长[1])
			                            秒 = int(工作时长[2])
			                            timee = 时 + 分 + 秒
			                            f = open(name + '.rtf', 'r')
			                            a = f.readlines()
			                            b = a[-1]
			                            b = b.split(',')
			                            c = b[2]
			                            c = c.split('当前资金:')
			                            c = c[1]
			                            c = list(c)
			                            if (len(c) == 1):
			                                c = [0, '时', 0, '分', 0, '秒']
			                            i = 0
			                            pw = b[1]
			                            pw = pw.split('密码:')
			                            pw = pw[1]
			                            import re
			                            def extract_time_units(lst):
			                                # 将列表转换为字符串
			                                lst_str = ''.join(map(str, lst))
			
			                                # 使用正则表达式匹配数字和单位
			                                pattern = r'(\d+)(时|分|秒)'
			                                matches = re.findall(pattern, lst_str)
			
			                                # 初始化变量
			                                时时 = None
			                                分分 = None
			                                秒秒 = None
			
			                                # 处理匹配结果
			                                for match in matches:
			                                    value, unit = match
			                                    if unit == '时':
			                                        时时 = int(value)
			                                    elif unit == '分':
			                                        分分 = int(value)
			                                    elif unit == '秒':
			                                        秒秒 = int(value)
			
			                                return 时时, 分分, 秒秒
			                            # 示例列表
			                            my_list = c
			                            # 提取时间单位
			                            时时, 分分, 秒秒 = extract_time_units(my_list)
			                            时 = 时 + int(时时)
			                            分 = int(分分) + 分
			                            秒 = int(秒秒) + 秒
			                            if (秒 > 59):
			                                秒 -= 60
			                                分 += 1
			                            if (分 > 59):
			                                分 -= 60
			                                时 += 1
			                            timme = str(时) + "时" + str(分) + "分" + str(秒) + "秒"
			                            工作时长[0] = 时
			                            工作时长[1] = 分
			                            工作时长[2] = 秒
			                            shenfen = "用户"
			                            tongy = "1"
			                            uuser = Account1(姓名, tongy, "退出登录", "操作:06运行{关闭窗口代码}")
			                            uuser.record_history()
			
			                            # 创建 Account 对象并记录
			                            user = Account(name, pw, timme, "退出登录", shenfen)
			                            user.record()
			                            tab_编号_助=0
			                            txt_编号_助=0
			                            txt_edit=[]
			                            tab=[]
			
			                        try:
			                            if txt_edit[txt_编号_助].get('1.0', tk.END) != 旬报:
			                                uuser = Account1(name, '1', "退出登录{正选择}", "操作:06运行{退出保存代码}")
			                                uuser.record_history()
			                                response = messagebox.askyesno(" 确认", "需要保存原文件吗？")
			                                if response:
			                                    save()
			                        except:
			                            pass
			                    except Exception as e:
			                        tb = traceback.extract_tb(sys.exc_info()[2])
			                        error_message = f"{e} (line {tb[-1].lineno})"
			                        print(f"报错: {error_message}")
			                    word.destroy()
			                    工作判 = False
			                    return

			                    if int(second)<10:

			                def on_configure(event):
			                    nonlocal last_state
			                    global 频道, tab_编号_助, txt_edit, tab,txt_编号_助
			                    try:
			                        current_state = word.wm_state()
			                        if current_state != last_state:
			                            if current_state == 'zoomed':
			                                # 获取屏幕的宽度
			                                screen_width = word.winfo_screenwidth()
			                                if 频道 == '00':
			                                    # 根据屏幕宽度设置 txt_edit 的宽度

			                                else:
			                                    return
			                            else:
			                                # 恢复默认宽度
			                                txt_edit[txt_编号_助].config(width=44)
			                            last_state = current_state
			                    except:
			                        pass

			                            subprocess.run(["open", file_path], check=True)
			                        else:  # Linux系统（Ubuntu/CentOS等）
			                            subprocess.run(["xdg-open", file_path], check=True)

			                    # print(Font)
			                    try:
			                        # 获取选中文本的位置
			                        a = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        b = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_LAST)
			
			                        # 定义一个辅助函数来获取或创建带有指定属性的字体
			                        def get_font_with_attributes(current_font, weight=None):
			                            return font.Font(family=current_font['family'],
			                                             size=current_font['size'],
			                                             weight=weight if weight else current_font['weight'],
			                                             slant=current_font['slant'])
			
			                        # 获取当前选中文本的所有标签
			                        current_tags = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_names(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			
			                        # 如果有现有标签，则从这些标签中获取字体属性
			                        for tag in current_tags:
			                            if tag != "bold":  # 忽略我们正在改变的标签
			                                current_font = font.Font(font=txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_cget(tag, "font"))
			                                break
			                        else:
			                            # 如果没有其他标签，使用默认字体
			                            current_font = font.Font(family=Font, size=ffont)
			                        # 检查是否已经应用了加粗
			                        if "bold" in current_tags:
			                            # 如果已应用加粗，则恢复到原始字体
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_remove("bold", a, b)
			                        else:
			                            # 创建新的加粗字体对象
			                            new_font = get_font_with_attributes(current_font, weight='bold')
			                            control_text_font_num += 1
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_add(f"bold_{control_text_font_num}", a, b)
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_config(f"bold_{control_text_font_num}", font=new_font)
			                    except tk.TclError:  # 当没有文本被选中时会抛出此异常
			                        return
			
			                def 斜体():
			                    global ffont, Font, txt_edit, tab_编号_助, tab, 姓名, control_text_font_num,txt_编号_助
			                    name = 姓名
			                    uuser = Account1(name, '1', "调整字形{斜体}", "操作:08编辑{改变文本字形}")
			                    uuser.record_history()
			                    try:
			                        # 获取选中文本的位置
			                        a = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        b = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_LAST)
			
			                        # 定义一个函数来获取或创建带有指定属性的字体
			                        def get_font_with_attributes(current_font, slant=None, weight=None):
			                            return font.Font(family=current_font['family'],
			                                             size=current_font['size'],
			                                             weight=weight if weight else current_font['weight'],
			                                             slant=slant if slant else current_font['slant'])
			
			                        # 获取当前选中文本的所有标签
			                        current_tags = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_names(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        # 如果已经应用了斜体，则移除斜体
			                        if "italic" in current_tags:
			                            # 获取现有斜体标签的字体属性并转换为直立
			                            current_font = font.Font(font=txt_edit[tab_编号_助].tag_cget("italic", "font"))
			                            new_font = get_font_with_attributes(current_font, slant='roman')
			                            txt_edit[tab_编号_助].tag_config("italic", font=new_font)
			                            txt_edit[tab_编号_助].tag_remove("italic", a, b)  # 移除斜体标签
			                        else:
			                            # 没有斜体标签时，添加斜体
			                            # 首先尝试从已有标签中获取字体属性
			                            for tag in current_tags:
			                                if tag != "italic":  # 忽略斜体标签，因为我们正在改变它
			                                    current_font = font.Font(font=txt_edit[tab_编号_助].tag_cget(tag, "font"))
			                                    break
			                            else:
			                                # 如果没有其他标签，使用默认字体
			                                current_font = font.Font(font=txt_edit[tab_编号_助].cget("font"))
			                            # 创建新的斜体字体对象
			                            control_text_font_num += 1
			                            new_font = get_font_with_attributes(current_font, slant='italic')
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_config(f"italic_{control_text_font_num}", font=new_font)
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_add(f"italic_{control_text_font_num}", a, b)  # 应用斜体标签
			
			                    except tk.TclError:  # 当没有文本被选中时会抛出此异常
			                        return
			
			                def control_text_font(text_font):
			                    global ffont, Font, txt_edit, tab_编号_助, tab, 姓名, Font, control_text_font_num,txt_编号_助
			                    try:
			                        control_text_font_num += 1
			                        a = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        b = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_LAST)
			                        new_font = font.Font(family=f"{text_font}")
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_add(f"new_font_{control_text_font_num}", a, b)
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_config(f"new_font_{control_text_font_num}", font=new_font)
			                        Font = f"{text_font}"
			                        name = 姓名
			                        uuser = Account1(name, '1', f"调整字体{Font}", "操作:08编辑{改变文本字体}")
			                        uuser.record_history()
			                    except:
			                        return

			                about_menu.add_command(label="宋体", command=lambda text_font='宋体': control_text_font(text_font),

			                def control_text_color(text_color):
			                    global Font, ffont, 姓名, txt_edit, tab_编号_助, tab, control_text_font_num,txt_编号_助
			                    name = 姓名
			                    uuser = Account1(name, '1', f"调整字色{text_color}", "操作:08编辑{改变文本字色}")
			                    uuser.record_history()
			                    try:
			                        start = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        end = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_LAST)
			                        # 创建或更新名为 "red" 的 tag，指定前景色为红色
			                        control_text_font_num += 1
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_config(f"color_{control_text_font_num}", foreground=f"{text_color}")
			                        # 应用 "red" tag 到选定的文本范围
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_add(f"color_{control_text_font_num}", start, end)
			                    except:
			                        return

			                def zih(text_size):
			                    global ffont, Font, txt_edit, tab_编号_助, tab, control_text_font_num,txt_编号_助
			                    try:
			                        # 获取选中文本
			                        start_idx = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_FIRST)
			                        end_idx = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].index(tk.SEL_LAST)
			                        selected_text = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].get(start_idx, end_idx)
			                        # 删除选中文本
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].delete(start_idx, end_idx)
			                        # 获取字体大小
			                        ffont = text_size  # 这里假设字体大小为ffont，实际应用中你需要从合适的地方获取，比如用户输入
			                        custom_font = font.Font(size=ffont)
			                        # 配置标签样式
			                        control_text_font_num += 1
			                        txt_edit[tab_编号_助].tag_config(f"custom_style_{control_text_font_num}", font=custom_font)
			                        # 重新插入文本并应用样式
			                        txt_edit[txt_编号_助].insert(start_idx, selected_text, f"custom_style_{control_text_font_num}")
			                        global 姓名
			                        name = 姓名
			                        uuser = Account1(name, '1', f"字号{ffont}", "操作:08编辑{调整字体大小}")
			                        uuser.record_history()
			                    except tk.TclError:
			                        pass
			
			                字号.add_command(label='7', command=lambda text_size='7': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='8', command=lambda text_size='8': zih(text_size))

			                字号.add_command(label='10', command=lambda text_size='10': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='11', command=lambda text_size='11': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='12', command=lambda text_size='12': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='13', command=lambda text_size='13': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='14', command=lambda text_size='14': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='16', command=lambda text_size='16': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='18', command=lambda text_size='18': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='20', command=lambda text_size='20': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='22', command=lambda text_size='22': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='25', command=lambda text_size='25': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='29', command=lambda text_size='29': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='34', command=lambda text_size='34': zih(text_size))
			                字号.add_command(label='40', command=lambda text_size='40': zih(text_size))
			                edit_menu.add_cascade(label="字号", menu=字号)

			                def control_text_place(text_place):
			                    global txt_edit, txt_编号_助, tab_编号_助,姓名
			                    try:
			                        try:
			                            #print(f'txt_编号_助:{txt_编号_助}')
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_remove("left", "1.0", "end")
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_remove("center", "1.0", "end")
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_remove("right", "1.0", "end")
			                            a = txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_ranges(tk.SEL)
			                            if not a:
			                                return
			                            #print(text_place)
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_add(f'{text_place}', *a)
			                            txt_edit[txt_编号_助].update_idletasks()#更新
			                            name = 姓名
			                            uuser = Account1(name, '1', f"调整文本排版{text_place}", "操作:08编辑{改变文本位置}")
			                            uuser.record_history()
			                        except tk.TclError:
			                            pass
			                    except Exception as e:
			                        # 打印错误信息和行号
			                        tb = traceback.extract_tb(sys.exc_info()[2])
			                        error_message = f"{e} (line {tb[-1].lineno})"
			                        print(f"报错: {error_message}")
			
			                # 定义不同的对齐标签(必写)
			                txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_configure("left", justify='left')
			                txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_configure("center", justify='center')
			                txt_edit[txt_编号_助].tag_configure("right", justify='right')
			                pb = tk.Menu(edit_menu, tearoff=0)
			                pb.add_command(label="三  ", command=lambda:control_text_place('left'))
			                pb.add_command(label=" 三 ", command=lambda:control_text_place('center'))

			                                import re
			
			                                def extract_time_units(lst):
			                                    # 将列表转换为字符串
			                                    lst_str = ''.join(map(str, lst))
			
			                                    # 使用正则表达式匹配数字和单位
			                                    pattern = r'(\d+)(时|分|秒)'
			                                    matches = re.findall(pattern, lst_str)
			
			                                    # 初始化变量
			                                    时时 = None
			                                    分分 = None
			                                    秒秒 = None
			
			                                    # 处理匹配结果
			                                    for match in matches:
			                                        value, unit = match
			                                        if unit == '时':
			                                            时时 = int(value)
			                                        elif unit == '分':
			                                            分分 = int(value)
			                                        elif unit == '秒':
			                                            秒秒 = int(value)
			
			                                    return 时时, 分分, 秒秒
			
			                                # 示例列表
			                                my_list = c
			                                # 提取时间单位
			                                时时, 分分, 秒秒 = extract_time_units(my_list)
			                                # 时+=360
			                                时 = 时 + int(时时)
			                                分 = int(分分) + 分
			                                秒 = int(秒秒) + 秒
			                                if (秒 > 59):
			                                    秒 -= 60
			                                    分 += 1
			                                if (分 > 59):
			                                    分 -= 60
			                                    时 += 1
			
			                                timme = str(时) + "时" + str(分) + "分" + str(秒) + "秒"
			                                work_时间 = timme
			                                
			                                label_work_时间.place(x=60, y=117)
			                                label_work_时间.config(text=f'办公时长:{work_时间}', font=('微软雅黑', 11))
